(declare-fun i_loop () (_ BitVec 22))
(declare-fun i-loop () Int)
(assert (and (> i-loop 0) (< i-loop 21)))
(assert (= ((_ int2bv 22) i-loop) i_loop))
(define-fun getbit ((x (_ BitVec 22)) (index (_ BitVec 22))) (_ BitVec 1)
	((_ extract 0 0) (bvlshr x index)))

(define-fun loopConV ((x (_ BitVec 22))) Bool
	(and
		(= (getbit x i_loop) ((_ extract 21 21) x)) ;; k+1 ~ i_loop
		(= (getbit (bvshl x (_ bv1 22)) i_loop) ((_ extract 20 20) x)))) ;; k ~ i_loop-1

(define-fun loopConF ((x (_ BitVec 22))) Bool
	(= (getbit x i_loop) ((_ extract 21 21) x))) ;; k+1 ~ i_loop

(define-fun next ((fap (_ BitVec 22)) (A (_ BitVec 22))) Bool
    (and
    	(= ((_ extract 20 0) fap) ((_ extract 21 1) A))
		(loopConF fap)))
		
(define-fun yesterday ((fap (_ BitVec 22)) (A (_ BitVec 22))) Bool
    (= fap (bvshl A (_ bv1 22))))
		
(define-fun zeta ((fap (_ BitVec 22)) (A (_ BitVec 22))) Bool
    (= fap (bvor (bvshl A (_ bv1 22)) (_ bv1 22))))

(define-fun until ((fap (_ BitVec 22)) (A (_ BitVec 22)) (B (_ BitVec 22))) Bool
	(and
		(= ((_ extract 20 0) fap) (bvor ((_ extract 20 0) B) (bvand ((_ extract 20 0) A) ((_ extract 21 1) fap))))
		(= #b1 (bvor ((_ extract 21 21) A) ((_ extract 21 21) B) (bvnot ((_ extract 21 21) fap))))
		(= #b1 (bvor (bvnot ((_ extract 21 21) B)) ((_ extract 21 21) fap)))
		(loopConF fap)
		(or (= #b0 ((_ extract 21 21) fap))
			(bvugt B (bvshl (_ bv1 22) i_loop)))))

(define-fun release ((fap (_ BitVec 22)) (A (_ BitVec 22)) (B (_ BitVec 22))) Bool
	(until (bvnot fap) (bvnot A) (bvnot B)))

(define-fun since ((fap (_ BitVec 22)) (A (_ BitVec 22)) (B (_ BitVec 22))) Bool
	(and
		(= ((_ extract 0 0) fap) ((_ extract 0 0) B) )
		(= ((_ extract 21 1) fap) (bvor ((_ extract 21 1) B) (bvand ((_ extract 21 1) A) ((_ extract 20 0) fap))))))

(define-fun trigger ((fap (_ BitVec 22)) (A (_ BitVec 22)) (B (_ BitVec 22))) Bool
	(since (bvnot fap) (bvnot A) (bvnot B)))

(define-fun alw ((fap (_ BitVec 22)) (A (_ BitVec 22))) Bool
	(= fap ((_ repeat 22) (bvredand A))))

(define-fun som ((fap (_ BitVec 22)) (A (_ BitVec 22))) Bool
	(= fap ((_ repeat 22) (bvredor A))))

(define-fun alwf ((fap (_ BitVec 22)) (A (_ BitVec 22))) Bool
	(until (bvnot fap) #b1111111111111111111111 (bvnot A)))

(define-fun alwp ((fap (_ BitVec 22)) (A (_ BitVec 22))) Bool
    (since (bvnot fap) #b1111111111111111111111 (bvnot A)))

(define-fun somp ((fap (_ BitVec 22)) (A (_ BitVec 22))) Bool
    (since fap #b1111111111111111111111 A))

(define-fun somf ((fap (_ BitVec 22)) (A (_ BitVec 22))) Bool
	(until fap #b1111111111111111111111 A))

(define-fun bviff ((A (_ BitVec 22)) (B (_ BitVec 22))) (_ BitVec 22)
    (bvxnor A B))
